economy_decisions = {
	refill_gold_reserve = {
		visible = {
			OR = {
				has_idea = no_gold_1
				has_idea = no_gold_2
				has_idea = no_gold_3
			}
		}
		cost = 250
		days_remove = 56
        remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = no_gold_1
				}
				remove_ideas = no_gold_1
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = no_gold_2
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = no_gold_2
					add_idea = no_gold_1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = no_gold_3
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = no_gold_3
					add_idea = no_gold_2
				}
			}
        }
	}
}
russian_gold_category = {
	evacuation_of_gold = {
		icon = GFX_decision_steel
		activation = {
			always = no
		}
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}
		is_good = yes
		cancel_trigger = {
			NOT = {
				252 = {
					is_controlled_by = RUS
				}
				249 = {
					is_controlled_by = RUS
				}
			}
		}
		days_mission_timeout = 60
		timeout_effect = {
			country_event = rcwgold.2
		}
	}
    unpack_gold_reserve = {
        visible = {
			check_variable = {
				ROOT.gold_reserve_var > 0
			}
			NOT = {
				original_tag = RUS
				has_active_mission = evacuation_of_gold_to_other_country
			}
        }
		cancel_trigger = {
			has_active_mission = evacuation_of_gold_to_other_country
		}
        icon = GFX_decision_steel
        fire_only_once = yes
        days_remove = 14
		cost = 25
        remove_effect = {
			set_country_flag = gold_reserve_unpacked
        }
    }
    stabilize_finiancial_system = {
        visible = {
			check_variable = {
				ROOT.gold_reserve_var > 0
				ROOT.stabilize_finiancial_system_var < 2
			}
			has_country_flag = gold_reserve_unpacked
			NOT = { has_active_mission = evacuation_of_gold_to_other_country }
        }
        icon = GFX_decision_generic_industry
        days_remove = 56
        remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = hyper_inflation_5
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = hyper_inflation_5
					add_idea = hyper_inflation_3
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = hyper_inflation_4
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = hyper_inflation_4
					add_idea = hyper_inflation_2
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = hyper_inflation_3
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = hyper_inflation_3
					add_idea = hyper_inflation_1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = hyper_inflation_2
				}
				remove_ideas = hyper_inflation_2
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = hyper_inflation_1
				}
				remove_ideas = hyper_inflation_1
				add_political_power = 75
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = CCA_no_money
				}
				remove_ideas = CCA_no_money
			}
			else = {
				add_political_power = 150
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_stability < 0.3
				}
				country_event = rcwgold.5
			}
			add_stability = 0.05
			add_political_power = 150
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = ROOT.gold_reserve_var
				value = 1
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = ROOT.stabilize_finiancial_system_var
				value = 1
			}
			russian_cw_set_gold_reserve_idea = yes
        }
    }
    buy_food = {
        visible = {
			check_variable = {
				ROOT.gold_reserve_var > 0
			}
			has_country_flag = gold_reserve_unpacked
			OR = {
				has_idea = foodstuffs_supply_crisis_1
				has_idea = foodstuffs_supply_crisis_2
				has_idea = foodstuffs_supply_crisis_3
				has_idea = foodstuffs_supply_crisis_4
				has_idea = foodstuffs_supply_crisis_5
			}
			NOT = { has_active_mission = evacuation_of_gold_to_other_country }
        }
        icon = GFX_decision_generic_industry
        days_remove = 120
        remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = foodstuffs_supply_crisis_5
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = foodstuffs_supply_crisis_5
					add_idea = foodstuffs_supply_crisis_3
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = foodstuffs_supply_crisis_4
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = foodstuffs_supply_crisis_4
					add_idea = foodstuffs_supply_crisis_2
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = foodstuffs_supply_crisis_3
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = foodstuffs_supply_crisis_3
					add_idea = foodstuffs_supply_crisis_1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = foodstuffs_supply_crisis_2
				}
				remove_ideas = foodstuffs_supply_crisis_2
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = foodstuffs_supply_crisis_1
				}
				remove_ideas = foodstuffs_supply_crisis_1
			}
			add_stability = 0.04
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = ROOT.gold_reserve_var
				value = 1
			}
			russian_cw_set_gold_reserve_idea = yes
        }
    }
    buy_trains = {
        visible = {
			check_variable = {
				ROOT.gold_reserve_var > 0
			}
			has_country_flag = gold_reserve_unpacked
			OR = {

				has_idea = collapse_of_railway_system_5
			}
			NOT = { has_active_mission = evacuation_of_gold_to_other_country }
        }
        icon = GFX_decision_generic_train
        days_remove = 150
        remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = collapse_of_railway_system_5
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = collapse_of_railway_system_5
					add_idea = collapse_of_railway_system_3
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = collapse_of_railway_system_4
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = collapse_of_railway_system_4
					add_idea = collapse_of_railway_system_2
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = collapse_of_railway_system_3
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = collapse_of_railway_system_3
					add_idea = collapse_of_railway_system_1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = collapse_of_railway_system_2
				}
				remove_ideas = collapse_of_railway_system_2
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = collapse_of_railway_system_1
				}
				remove_ideas = collapse_of_railway_system_1
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {

        }
    }
    buy_weapons = {
        visible = {
			check_variable = {
				ROOT.gold_reserve_var > 0
			}
			has_country_flag = gold_reserve_unpacked
			NOT = { has_active_mission = evacuation_of_gold_to_other_country }
        }
        available = {
			any_neighbor_country = {
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
			}
        }
        icon = generic_prepare_civil_war
        days_remove = 180
        complete_effect = {
			subtract_from_variable = {

				value = 1

        }
		remove_effect = {
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = infantry_equipment

			}

				type = support_equipment
				amount = 1000
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = motorized_equipment
				amount = 300
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = biplane_plane_airframe
				amount = 50
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = light_tank_chassis
				amount = 50
			}
		}
    }
    foreign_loans = {
        visible = {
			check_variable = {
				ROOT.gold_reserve_var > 0
			}
			has_country_flag = gold_reserve_unpacked
			NOT = { has_active_mission = evacuation_of_gold_to_other_country }
        }
        available = {
			any_other_country = {
				is_in_array = {
					array = ROOT.rcw_supported_states
					value = THIS.id
				}
			}
        }
        icon = GFX_decision_ger_mefo_bills
        days_remove = 90
        complete_effect = {
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = ROOT.gold_reserve_var
				value = 1
			}
			russian_cw_set_gold_reserve_idea = yes
        }
		remove_effect = {
			ROOT = {
				save_global_event_target_as = gold_loan_country
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_array = {
						array = THIS.rcw_supported_states
						value = ROOT.id
					}
				}
				country_event = rcwgold.6
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_array = {
						array = THIS.rcw_supported_states
						value = ROOT.id
					}
				}
				country_event = rcwgold.6
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_array = {
						array = THIS.rcw_supported_states
						value = ROOT.id
					}
				}
				country_event = rcwgold.6
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_array = {
						array = THIS.rcw_supported_states
						value = ROOT.id
					}
				}
				country_event = rcwgold.6
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_array = {
						array = THIS.rcw_supported_states
						value = ROOT.id
					}
				}
				country_event = rcwgold.6
			}
		}
    }
    evacuate_gold = {
        visible = {
			check_variable = {
				ROOT.gold_reserve_var > 0
			}
			has_war_with = RUS
			surrender_progress > 0.4
			NOT = {
				has_active_mission = evacuation_of_gold_to_other_country
				has_country_flag = gold_evacuation_country_choose
			}
        }
        available = {
			any_neighbor_country = {
				is_former_russian_empire_russian_country = yes
			}
        }
        icon = GFX_decision_steel
        days_remove = 5
		remove_effect = {
			country_event = rcwgold.7
			set_country_flag = gold_evacuation_country_choose
		}
    }
	evacuation_of_gold_to_other_country = {
		icon = GFX_decision_steel
		activation = {
			always = no
		}
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}
		is_good = yes
		cancel_trigger = {
			NOT = {
				is_neighbor_of = event_target:chosen_country_to_send_gold
			}
		}
		days_mission_timeout = 35
		timeout_effect = {
			event_target:chosen_country_to_send_gold = {
				country_event = rcwgold.8
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = event_target:chosen_country_to_send_gold.gold_reserve_var
				value = var:ROOT.gold_reserve_var
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = ROOT.gold_reserve_var
				value = var:ROOT.gold_reserve_var
			}
			russian_cw_set_gold_reserve_idea = yes
		}
	}
}
russia_in_ruins_category = {
	war_fatigue_growth = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_naval
		activation = {
			has_idea = russia_in_ruins_idea
			any_enemy_country = {
				is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes
			}
		}
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = {
					any_enemy_country = {
						is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		is_good = no
		days_mission_timeout = 140
		timeout_effect = {
			activate_mission = war_fatigue_growth
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = war_fatigue_1
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = war_fatigue_1
					add_idea = war_fatigue_2
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = war_fatigue_2
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = war_fatigue_2
					add_idea = war_fatigue_3
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = war_fatigue_3
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = war_fatigue_3
					add_idea = war_fatigue_4
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = war_fatigue_4
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = war_fatigue_4
					add_idea = war_fatigue_5
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = war_fatigue_5
				}
				remove_ideas = war_fatigue_5
				country_event = rcw.103
			}
		}
	}
	devastation_consequences = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_naval
		activation = {
			has_idea = russia_in_ruins_idea
			any_enemy_country = {
				is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes
			}
		}
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = {
					any_enemy_country = {
						is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		is_good = no
		days_mission_timeout = 56
		fixed_random_seed = no
		timeout_effect = {
			activate_mission = devastation_consequences
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					country_event = rcw.104
				}
				1 = {
					country_event = rcw.105
				}
				1 = {
					country_event = rcw.106
				}
				1 = {
					country_event = rcw.107
				}
				1 = {
					country_event = rcw.108
				}
				1 = {
					country_event = rcw.109
				}
			}
		}
	}
    move_to_peace = {
        fire_only_once = yes
        days_remove = 35
		cost = 10
		visible = {
			any_enemy_country = {
				is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes
			}
		}
        remove_effect = {
            add_stability = 0.01
			set_country_flag = move_to_peace_completed
        }
    }
    secret_negotiations = {
        fire_only_once = yes
        days_remove = 56
		cost = 25
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = move_to_peace_completed
			any_enemy_country = {
				is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes
			}
		}
        remove_effect = {
            add_stability = 0.03
			set_country_flag = secret_negotiations_completed
        }
    }
    prisoner_exchange = {
        fire_only_once = yes
        days_remove = 14
		cost = 10
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = secret_negotiations_completed
			any_enemy_country = {
				is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes
			}
		}
        remove_effect = {
			add_manpower = 200
			add_war_support = 0.02
			set_country_flag = prisoner_exchange_completed
        }
    }
    cease_fire = {
        fire_only_once = yes
        days_remove = 35
		cost = 25
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = prisoner_exchange_completed
			any_enemy_country = {
				is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes
			}
		}
        remove_effect = {
			add_stability = 0.02
			add_war_support = 0.02
			set_country_flag = cease_fire_completed
        }
    }
    delimitation = {
        fire_only_once = yes
        days_remove = 56
		cost = 25
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = cease_fire_completed
			any_enemy_country = {
				is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes
			}
		}
        remove_effect = {
			set_country_flag = delimitation_completed
        }
    }
	stop_fighting = {
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_remove = 35
		cost = 25
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = delimitation_completed
			any_enemy_country = {
				is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_former_russian_empire_russian_country = yes
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
				country_event = { id = rcw_all_rus_NA.25 hours = 1 }
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			country_event = rcw.103
		}
	}
	continue_fighting = {
		days_remove = 70
		cost = 300
		visible = {
			any_enemy_country = {
				is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes
			}
			OR = {
				has_idea = war_fatigue_2
				has_idea = war_fatigue_3
				has_idea = war_fatigue_4
				has_idea = war_fatigue_5				
			}
			check_variable = {
				ROOT.continue_fighting_var < 3
			}
		}
        remove_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { ROOT.continue_fighting_var = 1 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = war_fatigue_5
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = war_fatigue_5
					add_idea = war_fatigue_4
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = war_fatigue_4
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = war_fatigue_4
					add_idea = war_fatigue_3
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = war_fatigue_3
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = war_fatigue_3
					add_idea = war_fatigue_2
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = war_fatigue_2
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = war_fatigue_2
					add_idea = war_fatigue_1
				}
			}
        }
    }
}
operations = {
	repair_baltic_fleet_desision = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_naval
		available = {
			controls_state = 195
			controls_state = 1372
		}
		
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = baltic_fleet_in_exile
			OR = {
				owns_state = 219
				AND = {
					is_former_russian_empire_russian_country = yes
					OR = {
						controls_state = 195
						controls_state = 1372
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		cost = 50
		
		days_remove = 14
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			clr_global_flag = baltic_fleet_in_exile
			if = {
				limit = { has_dlc = "Man the Guns" }
				load_oob = RUS_1917_baltic_navy
				else = {
					load_oob = RUS_1917_baltic_navy_legacy

			}
		}
	}

russian_reunification_desisions = {
	national_assembly_desision = {
		icon = generic_ignite_civil_war
		available = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = RCW_Allrussian_national_assembly }

rcw_intervention_desisions = {

	GER_establish_loyal_government_in_UKR = {

		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		allowed = {
				original_tag = GER
		}
		available = {
			OR = {
				UKR = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				is_neighbor_of = UKR
				any_country = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					is_neighbor_of = UKR
				}
			}
			UKR = {
				exists = yes
				NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				NOT = { has_government = radical_socialism }
				NOT = { has_government = communism }
				NOT = { has_government = authoritarism }
				NOT = { has_government = despotism }
				NOT = { has_government = fascism }
				NOT = { has_government = national_syndicalism }
				OR = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					is_subject = no
				}
			}
			RUS = {

			NOT = { has_global_flag = UKR_communist_peace_fired }

			UKR = { is_subject = no }
			FRT = { NOT = { is_subject_of = RUS } }
			GRG = { NOT = { is_subject_of = RUS } }
		}

			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					AND = {
						tag = RUS
						surrender_progress > 0.2
						UKR = { surrender_progress < 0.1 }
					}
					AND = {
						tag = UKR
						RUS = { surrender_progress > 0.2 }
					}
				}
			}

			}

		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { tag = UKR }
				RUS = { country_event = { id = ukraine.59 days = 1 } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { tag = RUS }
				UKR = { country_event = { id = ukraine.59 days = 1 } }
